<pr_description>
[BUG] SQS: JSON 1.0 requests to /{accountId}/{queueName} are not routed correctly
 ## Service

  SQS

  ## AWS API Action

  SendMessage, GetQueueAttributes (and other JSON 1.0 SQS operations)

  ## Expected behavior

  SQS operations succeed normally — messages are enqueued and attributes are returned.

  ## Actual behavior

  Requests are routed to S3Controller instead of the SQS handler, resulting in an
  XML error response such as:

  ```xml
  <Error><Code>NoSuchBucket</Code><Message>The specified bucket does not exist</Message></Error>

  Reproduction

  # Using aws-sdk-sqs gem >= 1.71 (Ruby) or any SDK that sends JSON 1.0 SQS
  # requests to the queue-URL path rather than POST /

> more test.rb
require "aws-sdk-sqs"

  client = Aws::SQS::Client.new(
    region: "us-east-1",
    endpoint: "http://localhost:4566",
    credentials: Aws::Credentials.new("fake", "fake")
  )

  # Create the FIFO queue
  resp = client.create_queue(
    queue_name: "test.fifo",
    attributes: { "FifoQueue" => "true" }
  )
  queue_url = resp.queue_url
  puts "Created queue: #{queue_url}"

  # Send a message — this triggers the JSON 1.0 path-routing bug
  resp = client.send_message(
    queue_url: queue_url,
    message_body: "hello from ruby",
    message_group_id: "group1",
    message_deduplication_id: "dedup1"
  )
  puts "Sent message: #{resp.message_id}"
test.rb (END)

 gem install aws-sdk-sqs
 ruby test.rb

  Environment

  - Floci version / image tag:  hectorvent/floci:latest
  - How you're running Floci (Docker / native / mvn quarkus:dev):  Docker

    37	    public Response handle(String action, JsonNode request, String region) throws Exception {

    65	    private Response handleCreateQueue(JsonNode request, String region) {
    66	        String queueName = request.path("QueueName").asText(null);
    67	        Map<String, String> attributes = jsonNodeToMap(request.path("Attributes"));
    68	        Queue queue = sqsService.createQueue(queueName, attributes, region);
    69	
    70	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    71	        response.put("QueueUrl", queue.getQueueUrl());
    72	        return Response.ok(response).build();
    73	    }

   102	    private Response handleGetQueueAttributes(JsonNode request, String region) {
   103	        String queueUrl = request.path("QueueUrl").asText(null);
   104	        List<String> attributeNames = new ArrayList<>();
   105	        JsonNode namesNode = request.path("AttributeNames");
   106	        if (namesNode.isArray()) {
   107	            for (JsonNode n : namesNode) {
   108	                attributeNames.add(n.asText());
   109	            }
   110	        }
   111	        if (attributeNames.isEmpty()) {
   112	            attributeNames.add("All");
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        Map<String, String> attributes = sqsService.getQueueAttributes(queueUrl, attributeNames, region);
   116	
   117	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   118	        ObjectNode attrsNode = response.putObject("Attributes");
   119	        for (var entry : attributes.entrySet()) {
   120	            attrsNode.put(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
   121	        }
   122	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   123	    }
   124	
   125	    private Response handleSendMessage(JsonNode request, String region) {
   126	        String queueUrl = request.path("QueueUrl").asText(null);
   127	        String messageBody = request.path("MessageBody").asText(null);
   128	        int delaySeconds = request.path("DelaySeconds").asInt(0);
   129	        String messageGroupId = request.path("MessageGroupId").asText(null);
   130	        String messageDeduplicationId = request.path("MessageDeduplicationId").asText(null);
   131	
   132	        Map<String, MessageAttributeValue> messageAttributes = new HashMap<>();
   133	        JsonNode attrsNode = request.path("MessageAttributes");
   134	        if (attrsNode.isObject()) {
   135	            attrsNode.fields().forEachRemaining(entry -> {
   136	                String name = entry.getKey();
   137	                String dataType = entry.getValue().path("DataType").asText(null);
   138	                String stringValue = entry.getValue().path("StringValue").asText(null);
   139	                if (dataType != null && stringValue != null) {
   140	                    messageAttributes.put(name, new MessageAttributeValue(stringValue, dataType));
   141	                }
   142	            });
   143	        }
   144	
   145	        Message msg = sqsService.sendMessage(queueUrl, messageBody, delaySeconds,
   146	                messageGroupId, messageDeduplicationId, messageAttributes, region);
   147	
   148	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   149	        response.put("MessageId", msg.getMessageId());
   150	        response.put("MD5OfMessageBody", msg.getMd5OfBody());
   151	        if (msg.getMd5OfMessageAttributes() != null) {
   152	            response.put("MD5OfMessageAttributes", msg.getMd5OfMessageAttributes());
   153	        }
   154	        if (msg.getSequenceNumber() > 0) {
   155	            response.put("SequenceNumber", String.valueOf(msg.getSequenceNumber()));
   156	        }
   157	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   158	    }
   159	
   160	    private Response handleReceiveMessage(JsonNode request, String region) {
   161	        String queueUrl = request.path("QueueUrl").asText(null);
   162	        int maxMessages = request.path("MaxNumberOfMessages").asInt(1);
   163	        int visibilityTimeout = request.path("VisibilityTimeout").asInt(-1);
   164	        int waitTimeSeconds = request.path("WaitTimeSeconds").asInt(0);
   165	
   166	        List<Message> messages = sqsService.receiveMessage(queueUrl, maxMessages,
   167	                visibilityTimeout, waitTimeSeconds, region);
   168	
   169	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   170	        ArrayNode messagesArray = response.putArray("Messages");
   171	        for (Message msg : messages) {
   172	            ObjectNode msgNode = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   173	            msgNode.put("MessageId", msg.getMessageId());
   174	            msgNode.put("ReceiptHandle", msg.getReceiptHandle());
   175	            msgNode.put("MD5OfBody", msg.getMd5OfBody());
   176	            if (msg.getMd5OfMessageAttributes() != null) {
   177	                msgNode.put("MD5OfMessageAttributes", msg.getMd5OfMessageAttributes());
   178	            }
   179	            msgNode.put("Body", msg.getBody());
   180	
   181	            ObjectNode attrs = msgNode.putObject("Attributes");
   182	            attrs.put("ApproximateReceiveCount", String.valueOf(msg.getReceiveCount()));
   183	            attrs.put("SentTimestamp", String.valueOf(msg.getSentTimestamp().toEpochMilli()));
   184	            if (msg.getMessageGroupId() != null) {
   185	                attrs.put("MessageGroupId", msg.getMessageGroupId());
   186	            }
   187	            if (msg.getSequenceNumber() > 0) {
   188	                attrs.put("SequenceNumber", String.valueOf(msg.getSequenceNumber()));
   189	            }
   190	            if (msg.getMessageDeduplicationId() != null) {
   191	                attrs.put("MessageDeduplicationId", msg.getMessageDeduplicationId());
   192	            }
   193	
   194	            if (msg.getMessageAttributes() != null && !msg.getMessageAttributes().isEmpty()) {
   195	                ObjectNode msgAttrs = msgNode.putObject("MessageAttributes");
   196	                for (var entry : msg.getMessageAttributes().entrySet()) {
   197	                    ObjectNode valNode = msgAttrs.putObject(entry.getKey());
   198	                    valNode.put("DataType", entry.getValue().getDataType());
   199	                    valNode.put("StringValue", entry.getValue().getStringValue());
   200	                }
   201	            }
   202	
   203	            messagesArray.add(msgNode);
   204	        }
   205	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   206	    }

   223	    private Response handleDeleteMessageBatch(JsonNode request, String region) {
   224	        String queueUrl = request.path("QueueUrl").asText(null);
   225	        JsonNode entries = request.path("Entries");
   226	
   227	        ArrayNode successful = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   228	        ArrayNode failed = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   229	
   230	        if (entries.isArray()) {
   231	            for (JsonNode entry : entries) {
   232	                String id = entry.path("Id").asText();
   233	                String receiptHandle = entry.path("ReceiptHandle").asText(null);
   234	                try {
   235	                    sqsService.deleteMessage(queueUrl, receiptHandle, region);
   236	                    ObjectNode success = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   237	                    success.put("Id", id);
   238	                    successful.add(success);
   239	                } catch (AwsException e) {
   240	                    ObjectNode fail = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   241	                    fail.put("Id", id);
   242	                    fail.put("Code", e.getErrorCode());
   243	                    fail.put("Message", e.getMessage());
   244	                    fail.put("SenderFault", true);
   245	                    failed.add(fail);
   246	                }
   247	            }
   248	        }
   249	
   250	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   251	        response.set("Successful", successful);
   252	        if (!failed.isEmpty()) {
   253	            response.set("Failed", failed);
   254	        }
   255	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   256	    }

    58	                             DynamoDbJsonHandler dynamoDbJsonHandler,
    59	                             DynamoDbStreamsJsonHandler dynamoDbStreamsJsonHandler,
    60	                             SqsJsonHandler sqsJsonHandler, SnsJsonHandler snsJsonHandler,
    61	                             StepFunctionsJsonHandler sfnJsonHandler,
    62	                             CloudWatchMetricsJsonHandler cloudWatchMetricsJsonHandler) {
    63	        this.objectMapper = objectMapper;
    64	        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
    65	        this.dynamoDbJsonHandler = dynamoDbJsonHandler;
    66	        this.dynamoDbStreamsJsonHandler = dynamoDbStreamsJsonHandler;
    67	        this.sqsJsonHandler = sqsJsonHandler;
    68	        this.snsJsonHandler = snsJsonHandler;
    69	        this.sfnJsonHandler = sfnJsonHandler;
    70	        this.cloudWatchMetricsJsonHandler = cloudWatchMetricsJsonHandler;
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    @POST
    74	    @Consumes("application/x-amz-json-1.0")
    75	    @Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
    76	    public Response handleJsonRequest(
    77	            @HeaderParam("X-Amz-Target") String target,
    78	            @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
    79	            String body) {
    80	
    81	        if (target == null) {
    82	            return null;
    83	        }
    84	
    85	        String prefix;
    86	        String action;
    87	        String serviceName;
    88	
    89	        if (target.startsWith(DYNAMODB_STREAMS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
    90	            prefix = DYNAMODB_STREAMS_TARGET_PREFIX;
    91	            action = target.substring(prefix.length());
    92	            serviceName = "DynamoDBStreams";
    93	        } else if (target.startsWith(DYNAMODB_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
    94	            prefix = DYNAMODB_TARGET_PREFIX;
    95	            action = target.substring(prefix.length());
    96	            serviceName = "DynamoDB";
    97	        } else if (target.startsWith(SQS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
    98	            prefix = SQS_TARGET_PREFIX;
    99	            action = target.substring(prefix.length());
   100	            serviceName = "SQS";
   101	        } else if (target.startsWith(SNS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   102	            prefix = SNS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   103	            action = target.substring(prefix.length());
   104	            serviceName = "SNS";
   105	        } else if (target.startsWith(STEPFUNCTIONS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   106	            prefix = STEPFUNCTIONS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   107	            action = target.substring(prefix.length());
   108	            serviceName = "StepFunctions";
   109	        } else if (target.startsWith(CLOUDWATCH_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   110	            prefix = CLOUDWATCH_TARGET_PREFIX;
   111	            action = target.substring(prefix.length());
   112	            serviceName = "CloudWatch";
   113	        } else {
   114	            return Response.status(400)
   115	                    .entity(new AwsErrorResponse("UnknownOperationException",
   116	                            "Unknown operation: " + target))
   117	                    .build();
   118	        }
   119	
   120	        LOG.debugv("{0} JSON action: {1}", serviceName, action);
   121	
   122	        try {
   123	            JsonNode request = objectMapper.readTree(body);
   124	            String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(httpHeaders);
   125	
   126	            return switch (serviceName) {
   127	                case "DynamoDB" -> dynamoDbJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   128	                case "DynamoDBStreams" -> dynamoDbStreamsJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   129	                case "SQS" -> sqsJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   130	                case "SNS" -> snsJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   131	                case "StepFunctions" -> sfnJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   132	                case "CloudWatch" -> cloudWatchMetricsJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   133	                default -> null;
   134	            };
   135	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   136	            return Response.status(e.getHttpStatus())
   137	                    .type(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
   138	                    .entity(new AwsErrorResponse(e.jsonType(), e.getMessage()))
   139	                    .build();
   140	        } catch (Exception e) {
   141	            LOG.error("Error processing " + serviceName + " JSON request", e);
   142	            return Response.status(500)
   143	                    .type(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
   144	                    .entity(new AwsErrorResponse("InternalServerError", e.getMessage()))
   145	                    .build();
   146	        }
   147	    }
   148	
   149	    /**
   150	     * Serializes a JsonNode to CBOR bytes, encoding fields named "Timestamp" with CBOR tag 1
   151	     * as required by the smithy-rpc-v2-cbor protocol specification.
   152	     */
   153	    private static byte[] nodeToSmithyCbor(JsonNode node) throws Exception {
   154	        ByteArrayOutputStream out = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
   155	        CBORFactory factory = (CBORFactory) CBOR_MAPPER.getFactory();
   156	        try (CBORGenerator gen = factory.createGenerator(out)) {
   157	            writeNodeToCbor(gen, node, null);
   158	        }
   159	        return out.toByteArray();
   160	    }
   161	
   162	    private static void writeNodeToCbor(CBORGenerator gen, JsonNode node, String fieldName) throws Exception {
   163	        if (node.isObject()) {
   164	            gen.writeStartObject();
   165	            Iterator<Map.Entry<String, JsonNode>> fields = node.fields();
   166	            while (fields.hasNext()) {
   167	                Map.Entry<String, JsonNode> entry = fields.next();
   168	                gen.writeFieldName(entry.getKey());
   169	                writeNodeToCbor(gen, entry.getValue(), entry.getKey());
   170	            }
   171	            gen.writeEndObject();
   172	        } else if (node.isArray()) {
   173	            gen.writeStartArray();
   174	            for (JsonNode item : node) {
   175	                writeNodeToCbor(gen, item, null);
   176	            }
   177	            gen.writeEndArray();
   178	        } else if ("Timestamp".equals(fieldName) && node.isNumber()) {
   179	            gen.writeTag(1);
   180	            gen.writeNumber(node.longValue());
   181	        } else if (node.isTextual()) {
   182	            gen.writeString(node.textValue());
   183	        } else if (node.isDouble() || node.isFloat()) {
   184	            gen.writeNumber(node.doubleValue());
   185	        } else if (node.isLong() || node.isInt()) {
   186	            gen.writeNumber(node.longValue());
   187	        } else if (node.isBoolean()) {
   188	            gen.writeBoolean(node.booleanValue());
   189	        } else if (node.isNull()) {
   190	            gen.writeNull();
   191	        } else {
   192	            gen.writeString(node.asText());
   193	        }
   194	    }
   195	
   196	    /**
   197	     * Handles AWS smithy-rpc-v2-cbor protocol requests.
   198	     * AWS SDK v2 sends to POST /service/{sdkId}/operation/{op}
   199	     * with Content-Type: application/cbor and no X-Amz-Target header.
   200	     * Supported services: DynamoDB, SQS, SNS, StepFunctions, CloudWatch.
   201	     */
   202	    @POST
   203	    @Path("service/{serviceId}/operation/{operation}")
   204	    @Consumes("application/cbor")
   205	    @Produces("application/cbor")
   206	    public Response handleSmithyRpcV2Cbor(
   207	            @PathParam("serviceId") String serviceId,
   208	            @PathParam("operation") String operation,
   209	            @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
   210	            byte[] body) {
   211	
   212	        LOG.debugv("Smithy RPC v2 CBOR: service={0}, operation={1}", serviceId, operation);
   213	
   214	        try {
   215	            JsonNode request = (body != null && body.length > 0)
   216	                    ? CBOR_MAPPER.readTree(body)
   217	                    : objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   218	            String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(httpHeaders);
   219	
   220	            Response delegated = dispatchCbor(serviceId, operation, request, region);
   221	            if (delegated == null) {
   222	                return Response.status(404).build();
   223	            }
   224	
   225	            byte[] cborBytes = nodeToSmithyCbor((JsonNode) delegated.getEntity());
   226	            return Response.status(delegated.getStatus())
   227	                    .header("Smithy-Protocol", "rpc-v2-cbor")
   228	                    .type("application/cbor")
   229	                    .entity(cborBytes)
   230	                    .build();
   231	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   232	            return cborErrorResponse(e, "Smithy-Protocol");
   233	        } catch (Exception e) {
   234	            LOG.error("Error processing Smithy CBOR request: " + serviceId + "." + operation, e);
   235	            return Response.status(500).build();
   236	        }
   237	    }
   238	
   239	    /**
   240	     * Handles AWS services that migrated to the smithy-rpc-v2-cbor protocol at root path.
   241	     * Fallback handler for X-Amz-Target based routing with CBOR body.
   242	     */
   243	    @POST
   244	    @Consumes("application/cbor")
   245	    @Produces("application/cbor")
   246	    public Response handleCborRequest(
   247	            @HeaderParam("X-Amz-Target") String target,
   248	            @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
   249	            byte[] body) {
   250	
   251	        if (target == null) {
   252	            return null;
   253	        }
   254	
   255	        String prefix;
   256	        String serviceName;
   257	
   258	        if (target.startsWith(DYNAMODB_STREAMS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   259	            prefix = DYNAMODB_STREAMS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   260	            serviceName = "DynamoDBStreams";
   261	        } else if (target.startsWith(DYNAMODB_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   262	            prefix = DYNAMODB_TARGET_PREFIX;
   263	            serviceName = "DynamoDB";
   264	        } else if (target.startsWith(SQS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   265	            prefix = SQS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   266	            serviceName = "SQS";
   267	        } else if (target.startsWith(SNS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   268	            prefix = SNS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   269	            serviceName = "SNS";
   270	        } else if (target.startsWith(STEPFUNCTIONS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   271	            prefix = STEPFUNCTIONS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   272	            serviceName = "StepFunctions";
   273	        } else if (target.startsWith(CLOUDWATCH_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   274	            prefix = CLOUDWATCH_TARGET_PREFIX;
   275	            serviceName = "CloudWatch";
   276	        } else {
   277	            return null;
   278	        }
   279	
   280	        String action = target.substring(prefix.length());
   281	        LOG.debugv("{0} CBOR action: {1}", serviceName, action);
   282	
   283	        try {
   284	            JsonNode request = (body != null && body.length > 0)
   285	                    ? CBOR_MAPPER.readTree(body)
   286	                    : objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   287	            String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(httpHeaders);
   288	
   289	            Response delegated = switch (serviceName) {
   290	                case "DynamoDB" -> dynamoDbJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   291	                case "DynamoDBStreams" -> dynamoDbStreamsJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   292	                case "SQS" -> sqsJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   293	                case "SNS" -> snsJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   294	                case "StepFunctions" -> sfnJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   295	                case "CloudWatch" -> cloudWatchMetricsJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   296	                default -> null;
   297	            };
   298	            if (delegated == null) {
   299	                return null;
   300	            }
   301	
   302	            byte[] cborBytes = nodeToSmithyCbor((JsonNode) delegated.getEntity());
   303	            return Response.status(delegated.getStatus())
   304	                    .header("smithy-protocol", "rpc-v2-cbor")
   305	                    .type("application/cbor")
   306	                    .entity(cborBytes)
   307	                    .build();
   308	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   309	            return cborErrorResponse(e, "smithy-protocol");
   310	        } catch (Exception e) {
   311	            LOG.error("Error processing CBOR request: " + serviceName + "." + action, e);
   312	            return Response.status(500).build();
   313	        }
   314	    }
   315	
   316	    /** Dispatches a CBOR request to the appropriate service handler by SDK service ID. */
   317	    private Response dispatchCbor(String serviceId, String operation, JsonNode request, String region) throws Exception {
   318	        return switch (serviceId) {
   319	            case "DynamoDB" -> dynamoDbJsonHandler.handle(operation, request, region);
   320	            case "DynamoDB Streams" -> dynamoDbStreamsJsonHandler.handle(operation, request, region);
   321	            case "SQS" -> sqsJsonHandler.handle(operation, request, region);
   322	            case "SNS" -> snsJsonHandler.handle(operation, request, region);
   323	            case "SFN" -> sfnJsonHandler.handle(operation, request, region);
   324	            case CLOUDWATCH_SERVICE_ID -> cloudWatchMetricsJsonHandler.handle(operation, request, region);
   325	            default -> null;
   326	        };
   327	    }
   328	
   329	    private Response cborErrorResponse(AwsException e, String protocolHeader) {
   330	        try {
   331	            byte[] errBytes = CBOR_MAPPER.writeValueAsBytes(
   332	                    new AwsErrorResponse(e.jsonType(), e.getMessage()));
   333	            return Response.status(e.getHttpStatus())
   334	                    .header(protocolHeader, "rpc-v2-cbor")
   335	                    .type("application/cbor")
   336	                    .entity(errBytes)
   337	                    .build();
   338	        } catch (Exception ex) {
   339	            return Response.status(e.getHttpStatus()).build();
   340	        }
   341	    }
   342	}

     1	package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.s3;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.ws.rs.container.ContainerRequestContext;
     4	import jakarta.ws.rs.container.ContainerRequestFilter;
     5	import jakarta.ws.rs.container.PreMatching;
     6	import jakarta.ws.rs.core.UriBuilder;
     7	import jakarta.ws.rs.ext.Provider;
     8	import java.net.URI;
     9	
    10	@Provider
    11	@PreMatching
    12	public class S3VirtualHostFilter implements ContainerRequestFilter {
    13	
    14	    @Override
    15	    public void filter(ContainerRequestContext requestContext) {
    16	        String host = requestContext.getHeaderString("Host");
    17	        if (host == null) return;
    18	
    19	        String bucket = extractBucket(host);
    20	        if (bucket == null) return;
    21	
    22	        URI uri = requestContext.getUriInfo().getRequestUri();
    23	        String path = uri.getRawPath();
    24	
    25	        // Rewrite path from /key to /bucket/key
    26	        String newPath = "/" + bucket + (path.startsWith("/") ? "" : "/") + path;
    27	
    28	        URI newUri = UriBuilder.fromUri(uri)
    29	                .replacePath(newPath)
    30	                .build();
    31	
    32	        requestContext.setRequestUri(newUri);
    33	    }
    34	
    35	    /**
    36	     * Extracts a bucket name from a virtual-hosted-style Host header.
    37	     *
    38	     * The first label of the hostname (before the first dot) is treated as the
    39	     * bucket name whenever the hostname contains at least one dot and is not an
    40	     * IP address. This works for any endpoint hostname — localhost, custom hosts,
    41	     * or S3-style domains — without requiring configuration.
    42	     *
    43	     * Note: AWS SDKs automatically fall back to path-style for bucket names that
    44	     * contain dots, so the first-label heuristic is sufficient.
    45	     *
    46	     * Returns null if the host does not match a virtual-hosted pattern.
    47	     */
    48	    static String extractBucket(String host) {
    49	        if (host == null) return null;
    50	
    51	        // Strip port if present
    52	        String hostname = host;
    53	        int colonIndex = hostname.lastIndexOf(':');
    54	        if (colonIndex > 0) {
    55	            String maybePart = hostname.substring(colonIndex + 1);
    56	            if (!maybePart.isEmpty() && maybePart.chars().allMatch(Character::isDigit)) {
    57	                hostname = hostname.substring(0, colonIndex);
    58	            }
    59	        }
    60	
    61	        // Need at least one dot for a subdomain to exist
    62	        int firstDot = hostname.indexOf('.');
    63	        if (firstDot <= 0) {
    64	            return null;
    65	        }
    66	
    67	        // Skip IPv4 addresses (e.g., 192.168.1.1)
    68	        if (isIpv4Address(hostname)) {
    69	            return null;
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        return hostname.substring(0, firstDot);
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    private static boolean isIpv4Address(String hostname) {
    76	        for (int i = 0; i < hostname.length(); i++) {
    77	            char c = hostname.charAt(i);
    78	            if (c != '.' && (c < '0' || c > '9')) {
    79	                return false;
    80	            }
    81	        }
    82	        return true;
    83	    }
    84	}

    42	/**
    43	 * S3 controller handling REST-style S3 API requests.
    44	 * Routes: /{bucket} for bucket ops, /{bucket}/{key+} for object ops.
    45	 */
    46	@Path("/")
    47	public class S3Controller {
    48

    51	    private static final DateTimeFormatter RFC_822 = DateTimeFormatter
    52	            .ofPattern("EEE, dd MMM yyyy HH:mm:ss z", Locale.US)
    53	            .withZone(ZoneId.of("GMT"));

    70	    @Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
    71	    public Response listBuckets(@HeaderParam("X-Amz-Target") String target) {
    72	        if (target != null) {
    73	            return null;
    74	        }
    75	        try {
    76	            List<Bucket> buckets = s3Service.listBuckets();
    77	            XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
    78	                    .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
    79	                    .start("ListAllMyBucketsResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
    80	                    .start("Owner")
    81	                    .elem("ID", "owner")
    82	                    .elem("DisplayName", "owner")
    83	                    .end("Owner")
    84	                    .start("Buckets");
    85	            for (Bucket b : buckets) {
    86	                xml.start("Bucket")
    87	                   .elem("Name", b.getName())
    88	                   .elem("CreationDate", ISO_FORMAT.format(b.getCreationDate()))
    89	                   .end("Bucket");
    90	            }
    91	            xml.end("Buckets").end("ListAllMyBucketsResult");
    92	            return Response.ok(xml.build()).build();
    93	        } catch (AwsException e) {
    94	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
    95	        }

   101	        try {

   104	            if (bucketRegion == null || bucketRegion.isBlank()) {

   115	    @PUT
   116	    @Path("/{bucket}")
   117	    public Response createBucket(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   118	                                  @Context UriInfo uriInfo,
   119	                                  @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
   120	                                  byte[] body) {
   121	        try {
   122	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "notification")) {
   123	                return handlePutBucketNotification(bucket, body);
   124	            }
   125	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "versioning")) {
   126	                return handlePutBucketVersioning(bucket, body);
   127	            }
   128	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "tagging")) {
   129	                return handlePutBucketTagging(bucket, body);
   130	            }
   131	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "object-lock")) {
   132	                return handlePutObjectLockConfiguration(bucket, body);
   133	            }
   134	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "policy")) {
   135	                s3Service.putBucketPolicy(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   136	                return Response.ok().build();
   137	            }
   138	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "cors")) {
   139	                s3Service.putBucketCors(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   140	                return Response.ok().build();
   141	            }
   142	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "lifecycle")) {
   143	                s3Service.putBucketLifecycle(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   144	                return Response.ok().build();
   145	            }
   146	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "acl")) {
   147	                s3Service.putBucketAcl(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   148	                return Response.ok().build();
   149	            }
   150	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "encryption")) {
   151	                s3Service.putBucketEncryption(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   152	                return Response.ok().build();
   153	            }
   154	
   155	            String locationConstraint = null;
   156	            if (body != null && body.length > 0) {
   157	                locationConstraint = XmlParser.extractFirst(new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8),
   158	                        "LocationConstraint", null);
   159	            }
   160	            if (locationConstraint != null) {
   161	                locationConstraint = locationConstraint.trim();
   162	                if (locationConstraint.isEmpty()) {
   163	                    locationConstraint = null;
   164	                } else if ("us-east-1".equalsIgnoreCase(locationConstraint)) {
   165	                    throw new AwsException("InvalidLocationConstraint",
   166	                            "The specified location-constraint is not valid.", 400);
   167	                }
   168	            }
   169	            String region = locationConstraint != null ? locationConstraint : regionResolver.resolveRegion(httpHeaders);
   170	            s3Service.createBucket(bucket, region);
   171	            String lockEnabled = httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-bucket-object-lock-enabled");
   172	            if ("true".equalsIgnoreCase(lockEnabled)) {
   173	                s3Service.putBucketVersioning(bucket, "Enabled");
   174	                s3Service.setBucketObjectLockEnabled(bucket);
   175	            }
   176	            return Response.ok()
   177	                    .header("Location", "/" + bucket)
   178	                    .build();
   179	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   180	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   181	        }
   182	    }
   183	
   184	    @DELETE
   185	    @Path("/{bucket}")
   186	    public Response deleteBucket(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   187	                                  @Context UriInfo uriInfo) {
   188	        try {
   189	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "tagging")) {
   190	                s3Service.deleteBucketTagging(bucket);
   191	                return Response.noContent().build();
   192	            }
   193	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "policy")) {
   194	                s3Service.deleteBucketPolicy(bucket);
   195	                return Response.noContent().build();
   196	            }
   197	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "cors")) {
   198	                s3Service.deleteBucketCors(bucket);
   199	                return Response.noContent().build();
   200	            }
   201	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "lifecycle")) {
   202	                s3Service.deleteBucketLifecycle(bucket);
   203	                return Response.noContent().build();
   204	            }
   205	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "encryption")) {
   206	                s3Service.deleteBucketEncryption(bucket);
   207	                return Response.noContent().build();
   208	            }
   209	            s3Service.deleteBucket(bucket);
   210	            return Response.noContent().build();
   211	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   212	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   213	        }
   214	    }

   291	        } catch (AwsException e) {

   300	    public Response putObject(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   301	                              @PathParam("key") String key,

    27	 * - SSM (AmazonSSM.*)
    28	 * - EventBridge (AmazonEventBridge.*)

    80	    @POST
    81	    @Consumes("application/x-amz-json-1.1")
    82	    @Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
    83	    public Response handle(
    84	            @HeaderParam("X-Amz-Target") String target,
    85	            @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
    86	            String body) {
    87	
    88	        if (target == null) {
    89	            return null;
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        String prefix;
    93	        String serviceName;
    94	
    95	        if (target.startsWith(SSM_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
    96	            prefix = SSM_TARGET_PREFIX;
    97	            serviceName = "SSM";
    98	        } else if (target.startsWith(EVENTBRIDGE_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
    99	            prefix = EVENTBRIDGE_TARGET_PREFIX;
   100	            serviceName = "EventBridge";
   101	        } else if (target.startsWith(LOGS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   102	            prefix = LOGS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   103	            serviceName = "Logs";
   104	        } else if (target.startsWith(SECRETS_MANAGER_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   105	            prefix = SECRETS_MANAGER_TARGET_PREFIX;
   106	            serviceName = "SecretsManager";
   107	        } else if (target.startsWith(KINESIS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   108	            prefix = KINESIS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   109	            serviceName = "Kinesis";
   110	        } else if (target.startsWith(APIGW_V2_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   111	            prefix = APIGW_V2_TARGET_PREFIX;
   112	            serviceName = "ApiGatewayV2";
   113	        } else if (target.startsWith(KMS_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   114	            prefix = KMS_TARGET_PREFIX;
   115	            serviceName = "KMS";
   116	        } else if (target.startsWith(COGNITO_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   117	            prefix = COGNITO_TARGET_PREFIX;
   118	            serviceName = "Cognito";
   119	        } else if (target.startsWith(ACM_TARGET_PREFIX)) {
   120	            prefix = ACM_TARGET_PREFIX;
   121	            serviceName = "ACM";
   122	        } else {
   123	            return Response.status(400)
   124	                    .entity(new AwsErrorResponse("UnknownOperationException",
   125	                            "Unknown operation: " + target))
   126	                    .build();
   127	        }
   128	
   129	        String action = target.substring(prefix.length());
   130	        LOG.infov("AwsJson11Controller {0} action: {1}", serviceName, action);
   131	
   132	        try {
   133	            JsonNode request = objectMapper.readTree(body);
   134	            String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(httpHeaders);
   135	
   136	            return switch (serviceName) {
   137	                case "SSM" -> ssmJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   138	                case "EventBridge" -> eventBridgeHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   139	                case "Logs" -> cloudWatchLogsHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   140	                case "SecretsManager" -> secretsManagerJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   141	                case "Kinesis" -> kinesisJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   142	                case "ApiGatewayV2" -> apigwV2JsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   143	                case "KMS" -> kmsJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   144	                case "Cognito" -> cognitoJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   145	                case "ACM" -> acmJsonHandler.handle(action, request, region);
   146	                default -> null;
   147	            };
   148	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   149	            return Response.status(e.getHttpStatus())
   150	                    .type(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
   151	                    .entity(new AwsErrorResponse(e.getErrorCode(), e.getMessage()))
   152	                    .build();
   153	        } catch (Exception e) {
   154	            LOG.errorf("Error processing %s request", serviceName, e);
   155	            return Response.status(500)
   156	                    .type(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
   157	                    .entity(new AwsErrorResponse("InternalServerError", e.getMessage()))
   158	                    .build();
   159	        }
   160	    }
   161	}

2026-05-30 06:20:34,012 - INFO - swea-agent-floci-io__floci-153 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the architecture better. There are separate controllers for different JSON protocols. The issue is:

1. `AwsJsonController` handles `application/x-amz-json-1.0` at `@Path("/")` 
2. `AwsJson11Controller` handles `application/x-amz-json-1.1` at `@Path("/")`
3. `S3Controller` handles REST-style S3 requests at `@Path("/")`

The problem described in the PR is that when SQS sends JSON 1.0 requests to `/{accountId}/{queueName}` instead of `POST /`, the request gets routed to `S3Controller` instead of the SQS handler because S3Controller's `@Path("/{bucket}")` or `@Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")` catches the path.

But wait, looking at the PR more carefully: the issue is about the SQS JSON 1.0 requests being sent to `/{accountId}/{queueName}` path. In the newer AWS SDK versions, SQS requests are sent to a path like `/{accountId}/{queueName}` with `X-Amz-Target` header. The `AwsJsonController` currently only handles `@Path("/")` (root path). So when a request comes to `/{accountId}/{queueName}`, it doesn't match the root path, and instead falls through to S3Controller.

    34	    public Response handle(String action, MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
    35	        LOG.debugv("SQS action: {0}", action);
    36	
    37	        return switch (action) {
    38	            case "CreateQueue" -> handleCreateQueue(params, region);
    39	            case "DeleteQueue" -> handleDeleteQueue(params, region);
    40	            case "ListQueues" -> handleListQueues(params, region);
    41	            case "GetQueueUrl" -> handleGetQueueUrl(params, region);
    42	            case "GetQueueAttributes" -> handleGetQueueAttributes(params, region);
    43	            case "SendMessage" -> handleSendMessage(params, region);
    44	            case "ReceiveMessage" -> handleReceiveMessage(params, region);
    45	            case "DeleteMessage" -> handleDeleteMessage(params, region);
    46	            case "DeleteMessageBatch" -> handleDeleteMessageBatch(params, region);
    47	            case "SendMessageBatch" -> handleSendMessageBatch(params, region);
    48	            case "ChangeMessageVisibility" -> handleChangeMessageVisibility(params, region);
    49	            case "ChangeMessageVisibilityBatch" -> handleChangeMessageVisibilityBatch(params, region);
    50	            case "SetQueueAttributes" -> handleSetQueueAttributes(params, region);
    51	            case "TagQueue" -> handleTagQueue(params, region);
    52	            case "UntagQueue" -> handleUntagQueue(params, region);
    53	            case "ListQueueTags" -> handleListQueueTags(params, region);
    54	            case "PurgeQueue" -> handlePurgeQueue(params, region);
    55	            case "ListDeadLetterSourceQueues" -> handleListDeadLetterSourceQueues(params, region);
    56	            case "StartMessageMoveTask" -> handleStartMessageMoveTask(params, region);
    57	            case "ListMessageMoveTasks" -> handleListMessageMoveTasks(params, region);
    58	            default -> AwsQueryResponse.error("UnsupportedOperation",
    59	                    "Operation " + action + " is not supported by SQS.", AwsNamespaces.SQS, 400);
    60	        };
    61	    }

    63	    private Response handleCreateQueue(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
    64	        String queueName = getParam(params, "QueueName");

    97	    private Response handleGetQueueAttributes(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
    98	        String queueUrl = getParam(params, "QueueUrl");
    99	        List<String> attributeNames = new ArrayList<>();
   100	        for (int i = 1; ; i++) {
   101	            String name = getParam(params, "AttributeName." + i);
   102	            if (name == null) break;
   103	            attributeNames.add(name);
   104	        }
   105	        if (attributeNames.isEmpty()) {
   106	            attributeNames.add("All");
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        Map<String, String> attributes = sqsService.getQueueAttributes(queueUrl, attributeNames, region);
   110	
   111	        var xml = new XmlBuilder();

   113	            xml.start("Attribute")
   114	               .elem("Name", entry.getKey())
   115	               .elem("Value", entry.getValue())
   116	               .end("Attribute");
   117	        }
   118	        return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelope("GetQueueAttributes", null, xml.build())).build();
   119	    }

   121	    private Response handleSendMessage(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
   122	        String queueUrl = getParam(params, "QueueUrl");
   123	        String body = getParam(params, "MessageBody");
   124	        int delaySeconds = getIntParam(params, "DelaySeconds", 0);
   125	        String messageGroupId = getParam(params, "MessageGroupId");
   126	        String messageDeduplicationId = getParam(params, "MessageDeduplicationId");
   127	
   128	        Map<String, MessageAttributeValue> messageAttributes = new HashMap<>();
   129	        for (int i = 1; ; i++) {
   130	            String name = getParam(params, "MessageAttribute." + i + ".Name");
   131	            if (name == null) break;
   132	            String dataType = getParam(params, "MessageAttribute." + i + ".Value.DataType");
   133	            String stringValue = getParam(params, "MessageAttribute." + i + ".Value.StringValue");
   134	            if (dataType != null && stringValue != null) {
   135	                messageAttributes.put(name, new MessageAttributeValue(stringValue, dataType));
   136	            }
   137	        }
   138	
   139	        Message msg = sqsService.sendMessage(queueUrl, body, delaySeconds, messageGroupId, messageDeduplicationId, messageAttributes, region);
   140	
   141	        var xml = new XmlBuilder()
   142	                .elem("MessageId", msg.getMessageId())
   143	                .elem("MD5OfMessageBody", msg.getMd5OfBody());
   144	        if (msg.getMd5OfMessageAttributes() != null) {
   145	            xml.elem("MD5OfMessageAttributes", msg.getMd5OfMessageAttributes());
   146	        }
   147	        if (msg.getSequenceNumber() > 0) {
   148	            xml.elem("SequenceNumber", msg.getSequenceNumber());
   149	        }
   150	        return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelope("SendMessage", null, xml.build())).build();
   151	    }
   152	
   153	    private Response handleReceiveMessage(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
   154	        String queueUrl = getParam(params, "QueueUrl");
   155	        int maxMessages = getIntParam(params, "MaxNumberOfMessages", 1);
   156	        int visibilityTimeout = getIntParam(params, "VisibilityTimeout", -1);
   157	        int waitTimeSeconds = getIntParam(params, "WaitTimeSeconds", 0);
   158	
   159	        List<Message> messages = sqsService.receiveMessage(queueUrl, maxMessages, visibilityTimeout, waitTimeSeconds, region);
   160	
   161	        var xml = new XmlBuilder();
   162	        for (Message msg : messages) {
   163	            xml.start("Message")
   164	               .elem("MessageId", msg.getMessageId())
   165	               .elem("ReceiptHandle", msg.getReceiptHandle())
   166	               .elem("MD5OfBody", msg.getMd5OfBody());
   167	            if (msg.getMd5OfMessageAttributes() != null) {
   168	                xml.elem("MD5OfMessageAttributes", msg.getMd5OfMessageAttributes());
   169	            }
   170	            xml.elem("Body", msg.getBody())
   171	               .start("Attribute").elem("Name", "ApproximateReceiveCount")
   172	                 .elem("Value", String.valueOf(msg.getReceiveCount())).end("Attribute")
   173	               .start("Attribute").elem("Name", "SentTimestamp")
   174	                 .elem("Value", String.valueOf(msg.getSentTimestamp().toEpochMilli())).end("Attribute");
   175	            if (msg.getMessageGroupId() != null) {
   176	                xml.start("Attribute").elem("Name", "MessageGroupId")
   177	                   .elem("Value", msg.getMessageGroupId()).end("Attribute");
   178	            }
   179	            if (msg.getSequenceNumber() > 0) {
   180	                xml.start("Attribute").elem("Name", "SequenceNumber")
   181	                   .elem("Value", String.valueOf(msg.getSequenceNumber())).end("Attribute");
   182	            }
   183	            if (msg.getMessageDeduplicationId() != null) {
   184	                xml.start("Attribute").elem("Name", "MessageDeduplicationId")
   185	                   .elem("Value", msg.getMessageDeduplicationId()).end("Attribute");
   186	            }
   187	            if (msg.getMessageAttributes() != null && !msg.getMessageAttributes().isEmpty()) {
   188	                for (var entry : msg.getMessageAttributes().entrySet()) {
   189	                    xml.start("MessageAttribute")
   190	                       .elem("Name", entry.getKey())
   191	                       .start("Value")
   192	                       .elem("DataType", entry.getValue().getDataType())
   193	                       .elem("StringValue", entry.getValue().getStringValue())
   194	                       .end("Value")
   195	                       .end("MessageAttribute");
   196	                }
   197	            }
   198	            xml.end("Message");
   199	        }
   200	        return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelope("ReceiveMessage", null, xml.build())).build();
   201	    }

   218	    private Response handleDeleteMessageBatch(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
   219	        String queueUrl = getParam(params, "QueueUrl");
   220	        var xml = new XmlBuilder();
   221	
   222	        for (int i = 1; ; i++) {
   223	            String id = getParam(params, "DeleteMessageBatchRequestEntry." + i + ".Id");
   224	            if (id == null) break;
   225	            String receiptHandle = getParam(params, "DeleteMessageBatchRequestEntry." + i + ".ReceiptHandle");
   226	            try {
   227	                sqsService.deleteMessage(queueUrl, receiptHandle, region);
   228	                xml.start("DeleteMessageBatchResultEntry").elem("Id", id).end("DeleteMessageBatchResultEntry");
   229	            } catch (AwsException e) {
   230	                xml.start("BatchResultErrorEntry")
   231	                   .elem("Id", id)
   232	                   .elem("Code", e.getErrorCode())
   233	                   .elem("Message", e.getMessage())
   234	                   .elem("SenderFault", "true")
   235	                   .end("BatchResultErrorEntry");
   236	            }
   237	        }
   238	
   239	        return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelope("DeleteMessageBatch", null, xml.build())).build();
   240	    }

   242	    private Response handleSendMessageBatch(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
   243	        String queueUrl = getParam(params, "QueueUrl");
   244	        var xml = new XmlBuilder();
   245	
   246	        for (int i = 1; ; i++) {
   247	            String id = getParam(params, "SendMessageBatchRequestEntry." + i + ".Id");
   248	            if (id == null) break;
   249	            String body = getParam(params, "SendMessageBatchRequestEntry." + i + ".MessageBody");
   250	            int delaySeconds = getIntParam(params, "SendMessageBatchRequestEntry." + i + ".DelaySeconds", 0);
   251	            String messageGroupId = getParam(params, "SendMessageBatchRequestEntry." + i + ".MessageGroupId");
   252	            String messageDeduplicationId = getParam(params, "SendMessageBatchRequestEntry." + i + ".MessageDeduplicationId");
   253	
   254	            Map<String, MessageAttributeValue> messageAttributes = new HashMap<>();
   255	            for (int j = 1; ; j++) {
   256	                String name = getParam(params, "SendMessageBatchRequestEntry." + i + ".MessageAttribute." + j + ".Name");
   257	                if (name == null) break;
   258	                String dataType = getParam(params, "SendMessageBatchRequestEntry." + i + ".MessageAttribute." + j + ".Value.DataType");
   259	                String stringValue = getParam(params, "SendMessageBatchRequestEntry." + i + ".MessageAttribute." + j + ".Value.StringValue");
   260	                if (dataType != null && stringValue != null) {
   261	                    messageAttributes.put(name, new MessageAttributeValue(stringValue, dataType));
   262	                }
   263	            }
   264	
   265	            try {
   266	                var msg = sqsService.sendMessage(queueUrl, body, delaySeconds, messageGroupId, messageDeduplicationId, messageAttributes, region);

   268	                   .elem("Id", id)
   269	                   .elem("MessageId", msg.getMessageId())
   270	                   .elem("MD5OfMessageBody", msg.getMd5OfBody());
   271	                if (msg.getSequenceNumber() > 0) {
   272	                    xml.elem("SequenceNumber", msg.getSequenceNumber());
   273	                }
   274	                xml.end("SendMessageBatchResultEntry");
   275	            } catch (AwsException e) {
   276	                xml.start("BatchResultErrorEntry")
   277	                   .elem("Id", id)
   278	                   .elem("Code", e.getErrorCode())
   279	                   .elem("Message", e.getMessage())
   280	                   .elem("SenderFault", "true")
   281	                   .end("BatchResultErrorEntry");
   282	            }
   283	        }
   284	
   285	        return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelope("SendMessageBatch", null, xml.build())).build();
   286	    }

    30	/**
    31	 * Generic dispatcher for all AWS services that use the Query Protocol (form-encoded POST, XML response).
    32	 * Routes requests to the appropriate service handler based on the service name extracted from the
    33	 * Authorization header's credential scope, falling back to action-name matching when no auth header
    34	 * is present.
    35	 *
    36	 * <p>Currently supported services:
    37	 * <ul>
    38	 *   <li>SQS — form-encoded query protocol</li>
    39	 *   <li>SNS — form-encoded query protocol</li>
    40	 *   <li>IAM — form-encoded query protocol (global service)</li>
    41	 *   <li>STS — form-encoded query protocol (global service)</li>
    42	 * </ul>
    43	 *
    44	 * @see AwsJsonController
    45	 */
    46	@Path("/")
    47	public class AwsQueryController {

    52	    private static final Pattern SERVICE_PATTERN =

   115	    public AwsQueryController(CloudFormationQueryHandler cloudFormationQueryHandler,
   116	                              ElastiCacheQueryHandler elastiCacheQueryHandler,
   117	                              RdsQueryHandler rdsQueryHandler,
   118	                              SqsQueryHandler sqsQueryHandler, SnsQueryHandler snsQueryHandler,
   119	                              SesQueryHandler sesQueryHandler,
   120	                              IamQueryHandler iamQueryHandler, StsQueryHandler stsQueryHandler,
   121	                              CloudWatchMetricsQueryHandler cloudWatchMetricsQueryHandler,
   122	                              RegionResolver regionResolver) {
   123	        this.cloudFormationQueryHandler = cloudFormationQueryHandler;
   124	        this.elastiCacheQueryHandler = elastiCacheQueryHandler;
   125	        this.rdsQueryHandler = rdsQueryHandler;
   126	        this.sqsQueryHandler = sqsQueryHandler;
   127	        this.snsQueryHandler = snsQueryHandler;
   128	        this.sesQueryHandler = sesQueryHandler;
   129	        this.iamQueryHandler = iamQueryHandler;
   130	        this.stsQueryHandler = stsQueryHandler;
   131	        this.cloudWatchMetricsQueryHandler = cloudWatchMetricsQueryHandler;
   132	        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    @POST
   136	    @Consumes(MediaType.APPLICATION_FORM_URLENCODED)
   137	    @Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
   138	    public Response dispatch(
   139	            @HeaderParam("Authorization") String authorization,
   140	            @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
   141	            MultivaluedMap<String, String> formParams) {
   142	
   143	        String action = formParams.getFirst("Action");
   144	        if (action == null) {
   145	            return null;
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        String service = resolveService(authorization, action);
   149	        LOG.debugv("Query protocol service={0} action={1}", service, action);
   150	
   151	        String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(httpHeaders);
   152	
   153	        return switch (service) {
   154	            case "sqs" -> sqsQueryHandler.handle(action, formParams, region);
   155	            case "sns" -> snsQueryHandler.handle(action, formParams, region);
   156	            case "iam" -> iamQueryHandler.handle(action, formParams);
   157	            case "sts" -> stsQueryHandler.handle(action, formParams);
   158	            case "elasticache" -> elastiCacheQueryHandler.handle(action, formParams);
   159	            case "rds" -> rdsQueryHandler.handle(action, formParams);
   160	            case "email" -> sesQueryHandler.handle(action, formParams, region);
   161	            case "monitoring" -> cloudWatchMetricsQueryHandler.handle(action, formParams, region);
   162	            case "cloudformation" -> cloudFormationQueryHandler.handle(action, formParams, region);
   163	            default -> xmlErrorResponse("UnknownService",
   164	                    "Unknown or unsupported service: " + service, 400);
   165	        };
   166	    }
   167	
   168	    /**
   169	     * Determines the target AWS service. Prefers the service name embedded in the
   170	     * Authorization header credential scope. Falls back to action-name lookup when
   171	     * the header is absent (e.g. raw HTTP testing without AWS SDK auth).
   172	     */
   173	    private static final Set<String> ELASTICACHE_ACTIONS = Set.of(
   174	            "ValidateIamAuthToken",
   175	            "CreateReplicationGroup", "DescribeReplicationGroups", "DeleteReplicationGroup",
   176	            "CreateUser", "DescribeUsers", "ModifyUser", "DeleteUser"
   177	    );
   178	
   179	    private static final Set<String> CLOUDWATCH_ACTIONS = Set.of(
   180	            "PutMetricData", "ListMetrics", "GetMetricStatistics", "GetMetricData"
   181	    );
   182	
   183	    private static final Set<String> RDS_ACTIONS = Set.of(
   184	            "CreateDBInstance", "DescribeDBInstances", "DeleteDBInstance",
   185	            "ModifyDBInstance", "RebootDBInstance",
   186	            "CreateDBCluster", "DescribeDBClusters", "DeleteDBCluster", "ModifyDBCluster",
   187	            "CreateDBParameterGroup", "DescribeDBParameterGroups",
   188	            "DeleteDBParameterGroup", "ModifyDBParameterGroup", "DescribeDBParameters"
   189	    );
   190	
   191	    private static final Set<String> CLOUDFORMATION_ACTIONS = Set.of(
   192	            "CreateStack", "DeleteStack", "UpdateStack", "DescribeStacks",
   193	            "ListStacks", "GetTemplate", "ValidateTemplate",
   194	            "CreateChangeSet", "DeleteChangeSet", "DescribeChangeSet", "ExecuteChangeSet", "ListChangeSets",
   195	            "DescribeStackEvents", "DescribeStackResources", "ListStackResources", "DescribeStackResource",
   196	            "SetStackPolicy", "GetStackPolicy", "ListStackSets", "DescribeStackSet", "CreateStackSet"
   197	    );
   198	
   199	    private static final Set<String> SES_ACTIONS = Set.of(
   200	            "VerifyEmailIdentity", "VerifyEmailAddress", "VerifyDomainIdentity",
   201	            "DeleteIdentity", "ListIdentities", "GetIdentityVerificationAttributes",
   202	            "SendEmail", "SendRawEmail", "GetSendQuota", "GetSendStatistics",
   203	            "GetAccountSendingEnabled", "ListVerifiedEmailAddresses", "DeleteVerifiedEmailAddress",
   204	            "SetIdentityNotificationTopic", "GetIdentityNotificationAttributes",
   205	            "GetIdentityDkimAttributes"
   206	    );
   207	
   208	    private static final Set<String> QUERY_PROTOCOL_SERVICES = Set.of("sqs", "sns", "iam", "sts", "elasticache", "rds", "monitoring", "cloudformation", "email");
   209	
   210	    private String resolveService(String authorization, String action) {
   211	        if (authorization != null && !authorization.isEmpty()) {
   212	            Matcher m = SERVICE_PATTERN.matcher(authorization);
   213	            if (m.find()) {
   214	                String svc = m.group(1).toLowerCase();
   215	                if (QUERY_PROTOCOL_SERVICES.contains(svc)) {
   216	                    return svc;
   217	                }
   218	            }
   219	        }
   220	        return inferServiceFromAction(action);
   221	    }
   222	
   223	    private String inferServiceFromAction(String action) {
   224	        if (STS_ACTIONS.contains(action)) {
   225	            return "sts";
   226	        }
   227	        if (IAM_ACTIONS.contains(action)) {
   228	            return "iam";
   229	        }
   230	        if (SNS_ACTIONS.contains(action)) {
   231	            return "sns";
   232	        }
   233	        if (ELASTICACHE_ACTIONS.contains(action)) {
   234	            return "elasticache";
   235	        }
   236	        if (RDS_ACTIONS.contains(action)) {
   237	            return "rds";
   238	        }
   239	        if (CLOUDWATCH_ACTIONS.contains(action)) {
   240	            return "monitoring";
   241	        }
   242	        if (CLOUDFORMATION_ACTIONS.contains(action)) {
   243	            return "cloudformation";
   244	        }
   245	        if (SES_ACTIONS.contains(action)) {
   246	            return "email";
   247	        }
   248	        // SQS actions are numerous and not enumerated — fall back to sqs only for
   249	        // requests that arrived without an Authorization header (raw/test clients)
   250	        return "sqs";
   251	    }
   252	
   253	    private Response xmlErrorResponse(String code, String message, int status) {
   254	        String xml = new XmlBuilder()
   255	                .start("ErrorResponse")
   256	                  .start("Error")
   257	                    .elem("Type", "Sender")
   258	                    .elem("Code", code)
   259	                    .elem("Message", message)
   260	                  .end("Error")
   261	                  .elem("RequestId", UUID.randomUUID().toString())
   262	                .end("ErrorResponse")
   263	                .build();
   264	        return Response.status(status).entity(xml).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML).build();
   265	    }
   266	}

2026-05-30 06:20:51,797 - INFO - swea-agent-floci-io__floci-153 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I have a good understanding. Let me check how the S3Controller routes requests. The problem is clear:

1. `AwsJsonController` handles `application/x-amz-json-1.0` at `@Path("/")` 
2. Newer AWS SDKs (like `aws-sdk-sqs` gem >= 1.71) send JSON 1.0 requests to `/{accountId}/{queueName}` path instead of `POST /`
3. S3Controller has `@Path("/")` with sub-resources like `@Path("/{bucket}")` and `@Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")` 
4. When a JSON 1.0 request arrives at path `/{accountId}/{queueName}`, the S3Controller's `@Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")` catches it, thinking it's an S3 object operation

The fix should be to add a path for the AwsJsonController that also catches `/{accountId}/{queueName}` style paths for SQS. Let me look at how the path routing works.

Let me check the S3Controller more carefully for how it handles paths

    71	    SqsService(StorageBackend<String, Queue> queueStore, StorageBackend<String, List<Message>> messageStore,
    72	               StorageBackend<String, Map<String, Long>> dedupStore,
    73	               int defaultVisibilityTimeout, int maxMessageSize, String baseUrl,
    74	               RegionResolver regionResolver) {

    86	    private void loadPersistedMessages() {
    87	        if (messageStore == null) {
    88	            return;
    89	        }
    90	        for (String key : messageStore.keys()) {
    91	            messageStore.get(key).ifPresent(msgs ->
    92	                    messagesByQueue.put(key, new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>(msgs)));
    93	        }
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    private void loadPersistedDedup() {
    97	        if (dedupStore == null) {
    98	            return;
    99	        }
   100	        Instant now = Instant.now();
   101	        for (String key : dedupStore.keys()) {
   102	            dedupStore.get(key).ifPresent(entries -> {
   103	                ConcurrentHashMap<String, Instant> active = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
   104	                entries.forEach((dedupId, expiryMs) -> {
   105	                    Instant expiry = Instant.ofEpochMilli(expiryMs);
   106	                    if (now.isBefore(expiry)) {
   107	                        active.put(dedupId, expiry);
   108	                    }
   109	                });
   110	                if (!active.isEmpty()) {
   111	                    deduplicationCache.put(key, active);
   112	                }
   113	            });
   114	        }
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    private void persistMessages(String storageKey) {
   118	        if (messageStore == null) {
   119	            return;
   120	        }
   121	
   122	        var messages = messagesByQueue.get(storageKey);
   123	        if (messages != null) {
   124	            // Weakly-consistent snapshot; messages modified concurrently may or may not appear.
   125	            messageStore.put(storageKey, new ArrayList<>(messages));
   126	        } else {
   127	            messageStore.delete(storageKey);
   128	        }
   129	    }
   130	
   131	    private void persistDedup(String storageKey) {
   132	        if (dedupStore == null) {
   133	            return;
   134	        }
   135	        var dedupMap = deduplicationCache.get(storageKey);
   136	        if (dedupMap != null && !dedupMap.isEmpty()) {
   137	            Map<String, Long> serializable = new HashMap<>();
   138	            dedupMap.forEach((id, expiry) -> serializable.put(id, expiry.toEpochMilli()));
   139	            dedupStore.put(storageKey, serializable);
   140	        } else {
   141	            dedupStore.delete(storageKey);
   142	        }
   143	    }

   145	    public Queue createQueue(String queueName, Map<String, String> attributes) {
   146	        return createQueue(queueName, attributes, regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   147	    }
   148	
   149	    public Queue createQueue(String queueName, Map<String, String> attributes, String region) {
   150	
   151	        boolean fifoRequested = attributes != null && "true".equalsIgnoreCase(attributes.get("FifoQueue"));
   152	        boolean hasFifoSuffix = queueName != null && queueName.endsWith(".fifo");
   153	        if (fifoRequested && !hasFifoSuffix) {
   154	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValue",
   155	                    "The name of a FIFO queue can only end with '.fifo'.", 400);
   156	        }
   157	        if (hasFifoSuffix && !fifoRequested) {
   158	            // Auto-set FifoQueue attribute when name ends with .fifo
   159	            attributes = attributes == null ? new HashMap<>() : new HashMap<>(attributes);
   160	            attributes.put("FifoQueue", "true");
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        String accountId = regionResolver.getAccountId();
   164	        String queueUrl = baseUrl + "/" + accountId + "/" + queueName;
   165	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, queueUrl);
   166	
   167	        // If queue already exists with same name, check for attribute conflicts
   168	        Queue existing = queueStore.get(storageKey).orElse(null);
   169	        if (existing != null) {
   170	            if (attributes != null && !attributes.isEmpty()) {
   171	                Set<String> readOnlyAttrs = Set.of("QueueArn", "CreatedTimestamp", "LastModifiedTimestamp",
   172	                        "ApproximateNumberOfMessages", "ApproximateNumberOfMessagesNotVisible",
   173	                        "ApproximateNumberOfMessagesDelayed");
   174	                for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : attributes.entrySet()) {
   175	                    if (readOnlyAttrs.contains(entry.getKey())) {
   176	                        continue;
   177	                    }
   178	                    String storedValue = existing.getAttributes().get(entry.getKey());
   179	                    if (storedValue != null && !storedValue.equals(entry.getValue())) {
   180	                        throw new AwsException("QueueAlreadyExists",
   181	                                "A queue already exists with the same name but different attributes.", 400);
   182	                    }
   183	                }
   184	            }
   185	            return existing;
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        Queue queue = new Queue(queueName, queueUrl);
   189	        if (attributes != null) {
   190	            queue.getAttributes().putAll(attributes);
   191	        }
   192	        // Set default attributes
   193	        queue.getAttributes().putIfAbsent("VisibilityTimeout", String.valueOf(defaultVisibilityTimeout));
   194	        queue.getAttributes().putIfAbsent("MaximumMessageSize", String.valueOf(maxMessageSize));
   195	        queue.getAttributes().putIfAbsent("DelaySeconds", "0");
   196	        queue.getAttributes().putIfAbsent("MessageRetentionPeriod", "345600");
   197	        if (queue.isFifo()) {
   198	            queue.getAttributes().putIfAbsent("ContentBasedDeduplication", "false");
   199	        }
   200	
   201	        queueStore.put(storageKey, queue);
   202	        messagesByQueue.put(storageKey, new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>());
   203	        LOG.infov("Created {0} queue: {1} in region {2}", queue.isFifo() ? "FIFO" : "standard", queueName, region);
   204	        return queue;
   205	    }

   207	    public void deleteQueue(String queueUrl) {
   208	        deleteQueue(queueUrl, regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   209	    }
   210	
   211	    public void deleteQueue(String queueUrl, String region) {
   212	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, queueUrl);
   213	        if (queueStore.get(storageKey).isEmpty()) {
   214	            throw new AwsException("AWS.SimpleQueueService.NonExistentQueue",
   215	                    "The specified queue does not exist.", 400);
   216	        }
   217	        queueStore.delete(storageKey);
   218	        messagesByQueue.remove(storageKey);
   219	        deduplicationCache.remove(storageKey);
   220	        if (messageStore != null) {
   221	            messageStore.delete(storageKey);
   222	        }
   223	        if (dedupStore != null) {
   224	            dedupStore.delete(storageKey);
   225	        }
   226	        LOG.infov("Deleted queue: {0}", queueUrl);
   227	    }

   229	    public List<Queue> listQueues(String namePrefix) {
   230	        return listQueues(namePrefix, regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   231	    }
   232	
   233	    public List<Queue> listQueues(String namePrefix, String region) {
   234	        String prefix = region + "::";
   235	        if (namePrefix == null || namePrefix.isEmpty()) {
   236	            return queueStore.scan(key -> key.startsWith(prefix));
   237	        }
   238	        return queueStore.scan(key -> {
   239	            if (!key.startsWith(prefix)) {
   240	                return false;
   241	            }
   242	            String queueUrl = key.substring(prefix.length());
   243	            String name = queueUrl.substring(queueUrl.lastIndexOf('/') + 1);
   244	            return name.startsWith(namePrefix);
   245	        });
   246	    }

   251	
   252	    public String getQueueUrl(String queueName, String region) {
   253	        String accountId = regionResolver.getAccountId();
   254	        String queueUrl = baseUrl + "/" + accountId + "/" + queueName;
   255	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, queueUrl);
   256	        if (queueStore.get(storageKey).isEmpty()) {
   257	            throw new AwsException("AWS.SimpleQueueService.NonExistentQueue",
   258	                    "The specified queue does not exist for this wsdl version.", 400);
   259	        }
   260	        return queueUrl;
   261	    }

   263	    public Map<String, String> getQueueAttributes(String queueUrl, List<String> attributeNames) {
   264	        return getQueueAttributes(queueUrl, attributeNames, regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   265	    }
   266	
   267	    public Map<String, String> getQueueAttributes(String queueUrl, List<String> attributeNames, String region) {
   268	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, queueUrl);
   269	        Queue queue = queueStore.get(storageKey)
   270	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("AWS.SimpleQueueService.NonExistentQueue",
   271	                        "The specified queue does not exist.", 400));
   272	
   273	        Map<String, String> attrs = new java.util.LinkedHashMap<>(queue.getAttributes());
   274	        // Add computed attributes
   275	        attrs.put("QueueArn", regionResolver.buildArn("sqs", region, queue.getQueueName()));
   276	        attrs.put("CreatedTimestamp", String.valueOf(queue.getCreatedTimestamp().getEpochSecond()));
   277	        attrs.put("LastModifiedTimestamp", String.valueOf(queue.getLastModifiedTimestamp().getEpochSecond()));
   278	
   279	        var messages = messagesByQueue.getOrDefault(storageKey, new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>());
   280	        long visible = 0, inFlight = 0;
   281	        for (Message m : messages) {
   282	            if (m.isVisible()) {
   283	                visible++;
   284	            } else {
   285	                inFlight++;
   286	            }
   287	        }
   288	        attrs.put("ApproximateNumberOfMessages", String.valueOf(visible));
   289	        attrs.put("ApproximateNumberOfMessagesNotVisible", String.valueOf(inFlight));
   290	
   291	        if (attributeNames == null || attributeNames.contains("All")) {

Now I have a clear understanding. The SQS queue URL is `{baseUrl}/{accountId}/{queueName}` (e.g., `http://localhost:4566/000000000000/test.fifo`). Newer AWS SDKs send JSON 1.0 requests to this path. The problem is that `AwsJsonController` only listens at `@Path("/")` and when a request comes to `/{accountId}/{queueName}`, the S3Controller catches it because it has `@Path("/{bucket}")` or `@Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")`.

Let me look at how to properly fix this. The solution should be to add a path pattern in `AwsJsonController` that handles SQS JSON requests sent to `/{accountId}/{queueName}`.

But wait, let me also check if there's a `@Path` annotation on the S3Controller that could be catching it:

Looking at S3Controller:
- `@Path("/")` on the class
- `@GET` without path for listBuckets
- `@HEAD @Path("/{bucket}")` for headBucket
- `@PUT @Path("/{bucket}")` for createBucket
- `@DELETE @Path("/{bucket}")` for deleteBucket
- `@GET @Path("/{bucket}")` for listObjects
- `@PUT @Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")` for putObject
- `@GET @Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")` for getObject
- etc.

The AwsJsonController:
- `@Path("/")` on the class
- `@POST @Consumes("application/x-amz-json-1.0")` for handleJsonRequest 

So when a POST request comes to `/{accountId}/{queueName}` with `Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.0`, it should match AwsJsonController if the path matches. But the path in AwsJsonController is just `@Path("/")`, and the POST handler doesn't have a sub-path annotation, so it only matches `POST /`. The request to `/{accountId}/{queueName}` would not match this.

The JAX-RS framework will try to match the path. Since `AwsJsonController` doesn't have a path for `/{accountId}/{queueName}`, and S3Controller doesn't have a POST handler for `/{bucket}/{key:.+}` that consumes JSON 1.0, but it might still catch the request. Now I see the issue clearly. The S3Controller has:
- `@POST @Path("/{bucket}")` for `handleBucketPost`
- `@POST @Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")` for `handleMultipartPost`

These catch the POST requests to paths like `/{accountId}/{queueName}`. The AwsJsonController only handles `@Path("/")` for JSON 1.0, so requests to `/{accountId}/{queueName}` with `application/x-amz-json-1.0` are not matched.

The fix should be to add a path handler in `AwsJsonController` that also matches `/{accountId}/{queueName}` for SQS JSON 1.0 requests. But we need to be careful: we don't want to break S3's actual POST operations. The distinction is the `Content-Type` header: SQS JSON 1.0 uses `application/x-amz-json-1.0`, while S3 uses various content types (XML, multipart/form-data, etc.).

Looking at the JAX-RS routing: The `@Consumes` annotation on `AwsJsonController.handleJsonRequest()` limits it to `application/x-amz-json-1.0`. The S3Controller methods don't have `@Consumes` annotations, so they'd match any content type. 

So the fix should be in the `AwsJsonController` - we need to add a method that handles `application/x-amz-json-1.0` requests on paths like `/{accountId}/{queueName}`.

But wait, I need to think about this more carefully. The path `/{accountId}/{queueName}` is really for the SQS service. The newer AWS SDKs send JSON 1.0 requests with `X-Amz-Target: AmazonSQS.SendMessage` etc. to the queue URL path rather than to `POST /`.

Let me verify by looking at what the AWS SDK does. The PR description says:
> Requests are routed to S3Controller instead of the SQS handler

So the fix should add a path handler to `AwsJsonController` that matches any path like `/{segment1}/{segment2}` for JSON 1.0 requests, or perhaps more specifically, we should add the path `/{accountId}/{queueName}`.

Actually, a cleaner approach might be to add a generic catch-all path in `AwsJsonController`. Let me check if there's a way to match any path.

Looking at the S3Controller more, let me also check the `AwsJsonController` for the CBOR path:

```java
@POST
@Path("service/{serviceId}/operation/{operation}")
@Consumes("application/cbor")
```

So the CBOR protocol uses `service/{sdkId}/operation/{op}` path. 

For the JSON 1.0 protocol with SQS path-based routing, the newer SDKs (like Ruby's aws-sdk-sqs >= 1.71) send requests to `/{accountId}/{queueName}` with `X-Amz-Target` header.

The fix should add a method like:

```java
@POST
@Path("/{accountId}/{queueName}")
@Consumes("application/x-amz-json-1.0")
@Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
public Response handleJsonRequestPath(...)
```

But we need to make sure this doesn't conflict with S3 routes. Since the S3Controller doesn't have `@Consumes` annotation restricting content types, the JAX-RS runtime should prefer the more specific match (with `@Consumes`). But actually, both could match. Let me think about this...

Actually, JAX-RS matching would give priority to the handler that has the `@Consumes` matching. If the Content-Type is `application/x-amz-json-1.0`, the AwsJsonController with `@Consumes("application/x-amz-json-1.0")` should match better than S3Controller which has no `@Consumes` restriction.

But there's another issue: the `AwsJsonController` already has `@Path("/")` on the class. If we add `@Path("/{accountId}/{queueName}")`, that would be a different path than `@Path("/")`. We need to either:
1. Add a separate controller method for the path-based routing
2. Change the class-level `@Path` to something broader

Let me look at how other controllers handle this pattern. Let me check the DynamoDB controller
